## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

532026-03-08T19:47:43.087603agentmessage-
I am thinking...: Now I have a comprehensive picture of all the relevant files. Let me organize the findings for the final answer.json.

The three-tier permission model (Viewer/Editor/Admin) in Grafana is implemented across these key files:

## 1. Role Definition/Mapping

### `pkg/apimachinery/identity/role_type.go`
- Defines `RoleType` string type
- Constants: `RoleNone="None"`, `RoleViewer="Viewer"`, `RoleEditor="Editor"`, `RoleAdmin="Admin"`
- `rolePrecedence` map: None=10, Viewer=20, Editor=30, Admin=40
- Methods: `IsValid()`, `Includes()` (precedence-based), `Children()`, `Parents()`, `UnmarshalText()`

### `pkg/services/org/model.go`
- Re-exports `RoleType` and role constants from identity package
- `type RoleType = identity.RoleType`

### `pkg/services/accesscontrol/roles.go`
- Defines role name prefixes: `BasicRolePrefix="basic:"`, `FixedRolePrefix="fixed:"`, `ManagedRolePrefix="managed:"`
- `BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()` — creates the in-memory map of Admin/Editor/Viewer/None/GrafanaAdmin → `RoleDTO` structs (empty permissions, populated later via `DeclareFixedRoles`)
- `ValidateBuiltInRoles()`, `ValidateFixedRole()`
- Fixed role DTOs (ldapReaderRole, orgUsersWriterRole, etc.)

### `pkg/services/accesscontrol/models.go`
- `Permission` struct: `{Action, Scope}`
- `ResourcePermission` struct: `{Actions, Scope, UserID, TeamID, BuiltInRole, IsInherited, ...}`
- `RoleRegistration` struct: `{Role RoleDTO, Grants []string, Exclude []string}`
- `BuiltInRolesWithParents()` — expands a role to include all parent roles using `org.RoleType.Parents()`
- `GetOrgRoles()` — returns the org roles for a user (including GrafanaAdmin if applicable)
- `ManagedBuiltInRoleName()` — generates names like `"managed:builtins:viewer:permissions"`
